## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Application {
        +apiVersion: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
        +kind: Application
        +metadata
        +spec
    }
    class Spec {
        +project: string
        +destination
        +source/sources
        +syncPolicy
    }
    class Destination {
        +name: string
        +namespace: string
        +server: string
    }
    class HelmSource {
        +repoURL: string
        +chart: string
        +targetRevision: string
        +helm
    }
    class GitSource {
        +path: string
        +repoURL: string
        +targetRevision: string
        +helm
    }
    class Helm {
        +valueFiles: array
        +parameters
    }
    Application --> Spec
    Spec --> Destination
    Spec --> HelmSource
    Spec --> GitSource
    HelmSource --> Helm
    GitSource --> Helm
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckEnabled
    CheckEnabled --> LoopClusters: enabled=true
    CheckEnabled --> [*]: enabled=false
    LoopClusters --> SetConfig
    SetConfig --> CreateMetadata
    CreateMetadata --> CheckSource
    CheckSource --> HelmSource: source=helm
    CheckSource --> GitSource: source=git
    HelmSource --> ApplySyncPolicy
    GitSource --> ApplySyncPolicy
    ApplySyncPolicy --> CreateResource
    CreateResource --> NextCluster: has more
    CreateResource --> [*]: complete
    NextCluster --> SetConfig
```
